<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">The Claude Agent SDK is available in multiple forms to suit different use cases:</p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold"><a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/agent-sdk/typescript">TypeScript SDK</a></strong> - For Node.js and web applications</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold"><a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/agent-sdk/python">Python SDK</a></strong> - For Python applications and data science</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold"><a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/agent-sdk/streaming-vs-single-mode">Streaming vs Single Mode</a></strong> - Understanding input modes and best practices</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="font-heading leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="why-use-the-claude-agent-sdk"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Built on top of the agent harness that powers Claude Code, the Claude Agent SDK provides all the building blocks you need to build production-ready agents.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Taking advantage of the work we&#x27;ve done on Claude Code including:</p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Context Management</strong>: Automatic compaction and context management to ensure your agent doesn&#x27;t run out of context.</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Rich tool ecosystem</strong>: File operations, code execution, web search, and MCP extensibility</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Advanced permissions</strong>: Fine-grained control over agent capabilities</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Production essentials</strong>: Built-in error handling, session management, and monitoring</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Optimized Claude integration</strong>: Automatic prompt caching and performance optimizations</li>
</ul>

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Here are some example agent types you can create:</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Coding agents:</strong></p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">SRE agents that diagnose and fix production issues</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Security review bots that audit code for vulnerabilities</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Oncall engineering assistants that triage incidents</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Code review agents that enforce style and best practices</li>
</ul>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Business agents:</strong></p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Legal assistants that review contracts and compliance</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Finance advisors that analyze reports and forecasts</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Customer support agents that resolve technical issues</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Content creation assistants for marketing teams</li>
</ul>

          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Core Concepts</div></div></h2>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="authentication"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Authentication</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">For basic authentication, retrieve an Claude API key from the <a class="inline-link" href="/">Claude Console</a> and set the <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">ANTHROPIC_API_KEY</code> environment variable.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">The SDK also supports authentication via third-party API providers:</p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Amazon Bedrock</strong>: Set <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">CLAUDE_CODE_USE_BEDROCK=1</code> environment variable and configure AWS credentials</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Google Vertex AI</strong>: Set <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">CLAUDE_CODE_USE_VERTEX=1</code> environment variable and configure Google Cloud credentials</li>
</ul>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">For detailed configuration instructions for third-party providers, see the <a class="inline-link" href="https://code.claude.com/docs/en/amazon-bedrock">Amazon Bedrock</a> and <a class="inline-link" href="https://code.claude.com/docs/en/google-vertex-ai">Google Vertex AI</a> documentation.</p>
<div class="flex w-full rounded-lg p-2 px-4 gap-1 items-start text-sm border-0.5 my-6 border-accent-secondary-100 bg-accent-secondary-100/10 callout"><div class="flex mr-2 shrink-0 pt-[1.375px] text-accent-secondary-100"><div class="flex items-center justify-center" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 2.5C14.1421 2.5 17.5 5.85786 17.5 10C17.5 14.1421 14.1421 17.5 10 17.5C5.85786 17.5 2.5 14.1421 2.5 10C2.5 5.85786 5.85786 2.5 10 2.5ZM10 3.5C6.41015 3.5 3.5 6.41015 3.5 10C3.5 13.5899 6.41015 16.5 10 16.5C13.5899 16.5 16.5 13.5899 16.5 10C16.5 6.41015 13.5899 3.5 10 3.5ZM10.1006 9.00977C10.3286 9.05629 10.5 9.25829 10.5 9.5V12.5H11.5C11.7761 12.5 12 12.7239 12 13C12 13.2761 11.7761 13.5 11.5 13.5H8.5C8.22386 13.5 8 13.2761 8 13C8 12.7239 8.22386 12.5 8.5 12.5H9.5V10H8.5C8.22386 10 8 9.77614 8 9.5C8 9.22386 8.22386 9 8.5 9H10L10.1006 9.00977ZM10 6.5C10.4142 6.5 10.75 6.83579 10.75 7.25C10.75 7.66421 10.4142 8 10 8C9.58579 8 9.25 7.66421 9.25 7.25C9.25 6.83579 9.58579 6.5 10 6.5Z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="grow min-w-0 leading-relaxed text-accent-secondary-000 [&amp;_li]:before:text-accent-secondary-000/60 [&amp;_blockquote]:border-l-accent-secondary-000/60 [&amp;_code]:text-accent-secondary-000 [&amp;_code]:bg-accent-secondary-000/10"><p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Unless previously approved, we do not allow third party developers to apply Claude.ai rate limits for their products, including agents built on the Claude Agent SDK. Please use the API key authentication methods described in this document instead.</p></div></div>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="full-claude-code-feature-support"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none

  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Full Claude Code Feature Support</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">The SDK provides access to all the default features available in Claude Code, leveraging the same file system-based configuration:</p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Subagents</strong>: Launch specialized agents stored as Markdown files in <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">./.claude/agents/</code></li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Agent Skills</strong>: Extend Claude with specialized capabilities stored as <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">SKILL.md</code> files in <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">./.claude/skills/</code></li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Hooks</strong>: Execute custom commands configured in <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">./.claude/settings.json</code> that respond to tool events</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Slash Commands</strong>: Use custom commands defined as Markdown files in <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">./.claude/commands/</code></li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Plugins</strong>: Load custom plugins programmatically using the <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">plugins</code> option to extend Claude Code with custom commands, agents, skills, hooks, and MCP servers. See <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/agent-sdk/plugins">Plugins</a> for details.</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Memory (CLAUDE.md)</strong>: Maintain project context through <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">CLAUDE.md</code> or <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">.claude/CLAUDE.md</code> files in your project directory, or <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">~/.claude/CLAUDE.md</code> for user-level instructions. To load these files, you must explicitly set <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">settingSources: [&#x27;project&#x27;]</code> (TypeScript) or <code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">setting_sources=[&quot;project&quot;]</code> (Python) in your options. See <a class="inline-link" href="/docs/en/agent-sdk/modifying-system-prompts#method-1-claudemd-files-project-level-instructions">Modifying system prompts</a> for details.</li>
</ul>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">These features work identically to their Claude Code counterparts by reading from the same file system locations.</p>

<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">System prompts define your agent&#x27;s role, expertise, and behavior. This is where you specify what kind of agent you&#x27;re building.</p>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="tool-permissions"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Tool Permissions</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Control which tools your agent can use with fine-grained permissions:</p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">allowedTools</code> - Explicitly allow specific tools</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">disallowedTools</code> - Block specific tools</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><code class="relative inline bg-bg-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-sm font-mono break-words box-decoration-clone">permissionMode</code> - Set overall permission strategy</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="model-context-protocol-mcp"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex

  justify-center
  relative

  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none

  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Model Context Protocol (MCP)</div></div></h3>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Extend your agents with custom tools and integrations through MCP servers. This allows you to connect to databases, APIs, and other external services.</p>
<h2 class="font-heading leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="building-with-the-claude-agent-sdk"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base
          duration-300
          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>Building with the Claude Agent SDK</div></div></h2>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">If you&#x27;re building coding agents powered by the Claude Agent SDK, please note that <strong class="font-semibold">Claude Code</strong> refers specifically to Anthropic&#x27;s official product including the CLI, VS Code extension, web experience, and future integrations we build.</p>
<h3 class="text-xl font-medium leading-[1.25] text-text-100"><div class="relative group pt-6 pb-2" id="for-partners-integrating-claude-agent-sdk"><div class="absolute hidden sm:block sm:-ml-8"><button class="inline-flex
  items-center
  justify-center
  relative
  shrink-0
  can-focus
  select-none
  disabled:pointer-events-none
  disabled:opacity-50
  disabled:shadow-none
  disabled:drop-shadow-none border-transparent
          transition
          font-base

          ease-[cubic-bezier(0.165,0.85,0.45,1)] h-6 w-6 rounded-md active:scale-95 absolute left-0 transform opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity duration-200 text-text-500 hover:text-text-100 Button_ghost__BUAoh" type="button" aria-label="Copy link to clipboard" title="Copy link to clipboard" data-state="closed"><div class="flex items-center justify-center inline" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0 inline" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M13.6229 9.64789C13.8798 9.54672 14.1701 9.6724 14.2714 9.92914L15.2792 12.4878C16.0889 14.5432 15.0788 16.8666 13.0233 17.6763C11.0323 18.4603 8.79012 17.5367 7.91585 15.6098L7.83577 15.4204L6.82795 12.8618C6.72674 12.6048 6.85325 12.3145 7.11018 12.2133C7.36701 12.1122 7.65732 12.2379 7.75862 12.4946L8.76645 15.0532C9.37368 16.5947 11.1156 17.3528 12.6571 16.7456C14.1986 16.1384 14.9557 14.3965 14.3485 12.8549L13.3407 10.2963C13.2395 10.0395 13.3661 9.74917 13.6229 9.64789ZM8.90024 7.20842C9.15717 7.10721 9.44747 7.23372 9.54868 7.49065L11.3817 12.143C11.4826 12.3998 11.3563 12.6903 11.0995 12.7915C10.8426 12.8925 10.5523 12.766 10.451 12.5092L8.61898 7.85686C8.5178 7.59999 8.64342 7.30969 8.90024 7.20842ZM7.16975 2.25331C9.17539 1.57852 11.3796 2.58838 12.1639 4.5795L13.1718 7.13811C13.273 7.39504 13.1465 7.68534 12.8895 7.78655C12.6327 7.88749 12.3423 7.76113 12.2411 7.50432L11.2333 4.94571C10.6259 3.40439 8.88406 2.6471 7.3426 3.25429C5.80118 3.86161 5.04399 5.60345 5.65118 7.14494L6.659 9.70355C6.76021 9.96048 6.6337 10.2508 6.37677 10.352C6.11988 10.4531 5.82952 10.3266 5.72833 10.0698L4.7205 7.51116C3.91111 5.45581 4.92107 3.13323 6.97639 2.32362L7.16975 2.25331Z"></path></svg></div></button></div><div>For partners integrating Claude Agent SDK:</div></div></h3>
<div class="flex w-full rounded-lg p-2 px-4 gap-1 items-start text-sm border-0.5 my-6 border-accent-secondary-100 bg-accent-secondary-100/10 callout"><div class="flex mr-2 shrink-0 pt-[1.375px] text-accent-secondary-100"><div class="flex items-center justify-center" style="width:20px;height:20px"><svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="currentColor" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="shrink-0" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M10 2.5C14.1421 2.5 17.5 5.85786 17.5 10C17.5 14.1421 14.1421 17.5 10 17.5C5.85786 17.5 2.5 14.1421 2.5 10C2.5 5.85786 5.85786 2.5 10 2.5ZM10 3.5C6.41015 3.5 3.5 6.41015 3.5 10C3.5 13.5899 6.41015 16.5 10 16.5C13.5899 16.5 16.5 13.5899 16.5 10C16.5 6.41015 13.5899 3.5 10 3.5ZM10.1006 9.00977C10.3286 9.05629 10.5 9.25829 10.5 9.5V12.5H11.5C11.7761 12.5 12 12.7239 12 13C12 13.2761 11.7761 13.5 11.5 13.5H8.5C8.22386 13.5 8 13.2761 8 13C8 12.7239 8.22386 12.5 8.5 12.5H9.5V10H8.5C8.22386 10 8 9.77614 8 9.5C8 9.22386 8.22386 9 8.5 9H10L10.1006 9.00977ZM10 6.5C10.4142 6.5 10.75 6.83579 10.75 7.25C10.75 7.66421 10.4142 8 10 8C9.58579 8 9.25 7.66421 9.25 7.25C9.25 6.83579 9.58579 6.5 10 6.5Z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="grow min-w-0 leading-relaxed text-accent-secondary-000 [&amp;_li]:before:text-accent-secondary-000/60 [&amp;_blockquote]:border-l-accent-secondary-000/60 [&amp;_code]:text-accent-secondary-000 [&amp;_code]:bg-accent-secondary-000/10"><p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">The use of Claude branding for products built on Claude is optional.</p></div></div>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">When referencing Claude in your agent selector or product:</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Allowed naming options:</strong></p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Claude Agent</strong> (preferred for dropdown menus)</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">Claude</strong> (when within a menu already labeled &quot;Agents&quot;)</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]"><strong class="font-semibold">{YourAgentName} Powered by Claude</strong> (if you have an existing agent name)</li>
</ul>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0"><strong class="font-semibold">Not permitted:</strong></p>
<ul class="list-none mb-4 pl-8 [&amp;_ul]:pl-8 [&amp;_ol]:pl-8">
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">&quot;Claude Code&quot; or &quot;Claude Code Agent&quot;</li>
<li class="mb-2 last:mb-0 relative before:absolute before:left-[-2rem] before:w-6 before:text-center [ul&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[&#x27;â€¢&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:before:content-[counter(item)&#x27;.&#x27;] [ol&gt;&amp;]:[counter-increment:item]">Claude Code-branded ASCII art or visual elements that mimic Claude Code</li>
</ul>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">Your product should maintain its own branding and not appear to be Claude Code or any Anthropic product.</p>
<p class="mb-4 last:mb-0">For questions about branding compliance or to discuss your product&#x27;s Claude integration, <a class="inline-link" href="https://claude.com/contact-sales">contact our sales team</a>.</p>
